<script>
function counterTnsNew() {
  const matchesLkuid = document.cookie.match(/(?<!\w)lkuid=([^;]*)/);
  const lkuid = matchesLkuid ? matchesLkuid[1] : '';
  const matchesSessionId = document.cookie.match(/(?<!\w)kommersantSessionId=([^;]*)/);
  let sessionId;
  if (matchesSessionId) {
    sessionId = matchesSessionId[1];
  } else {
    const size = 16;
    let seed = '';
    sessionId = '';
    for (let i = 48; i <= 122; i += (i === 57 ? 40 : 1)) {
      seed += String.fromCharCode(i);
    }
    for (let i = 0; i < size; i += 1) {
      sessionId += seed.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * seed.length));
    }
    document.cookie = 'kommersantSessionId=' + sessionId;
  }
  const idlc = window.doc && window.doc.id || null;
  const ver = 0;
  const type = (window.doc && window.doc.id) ? 4 : 0;
  let url = '//tns-counter.ru/e/ec01';
  url += '&cid=kommersant_ru';
  url += '&typ=1';
  url += '&tms=kommersant_ru';
  url += '&idc=155';
  url += '&uid=' + sessionId;
  url += '&hid=' + lkuid;
  url += idlc ? '&idlc=' + idlc : '';
  url += '&ver=' + ver;
  url += '&type=' + type;
  fetch(url, { credentials: 'include' }).catch(() => false);
}
counterTnsNew();
</script>

    var yaParams = {};
    window.kommersantAnalytics.rubrics && (yaParams.rubric = window.kommersantAnalytics.rubrics);
    window.kommersantAnalytics.publishing && (yaParams.publication = window.kommersantAnalytics.publishing);
    window.kommersantAnalytics.themes && (yaParams.theme = window.kommersantAnalytics.themes);
    window.kommersantAnalytics.themegroups && (yaParams.maintheme = window.kommersantAnalytics.themegroups);
    try {
      ym(153166, 'params', yaParams);
      ym(153166, 'hit', window.location.pathname + window.location.search + window.location.hash, {
        params: yaParams
      });
    } catch (ignore) {}
  })();

  (function () {
    try {
      ga('set', 'page', window.location.pathname + window.location.search + window.location.hash);
      ga('set', 'dimension1', window.kommersantAnalytics.rubrics || null);
      ga('set', 'dimension2', window.kommersantAnalytics.publishing || null);
      ga('set', 'dimension4', window.kommersantAnalytics.themes || null);
      ga('set', 'dimension5', window.kommersantAnalytics.themegroups || null);
      ga('set', 'dimension8', window.kommersantAnalytics.authors || null);
      ga('set', 'dimension6', window.kommersantAnalytics.audio || null);
      ga('set', 'dimension3', window.kommersantAnalytics.adblock || null);
      ga('set', 'dimension10', window.kommersantAnalytics.region || null);
      ga('send', 'pageview');
    } catch (ignore) {}
  })();

  counterTnsNew();

  counterTnsOld();


}
</script>
